#oofSrc='0423-0120' #Note Ta* of it. 
#oofSrc='0854+2006'

# Flux scalibration source
#fluxSrc='0423-0120'
fluxSrc = '0319+4130'
#fluxSrc = '2253+1608'
#fluxSrc = '1229+0203' # good if OOFing
#fluxSrc = "1058+0133"
#fluxSrc = '0854+2006' # good if not OOFing

# Avoid using pointing corrections when pointing source is in 
# key-hole (elev >~85 deg)
pointSrc="0237+2848"  # ptg 1
#pointSrc="0410+7656"  # ptg 2
#pointSrc="0738+1742"  # ptg 3 & 5
#pointSrc="0854+2006"  # ptg 4
#pointSrc="0927+3902"  # ptg 6

#pointSrc="1159+2914"  # source 3
#pointSrc="0237+2848" #s33 point 1, s34 point1
#pointSrc="0813+4813" #s33 point 2
#pointSrc="0741+3112" #s33 point 3
#pointSrc="0834+5534" #s33 point 4
#pointSrc="0956+2515" #s33 point 5
#pointSrc="1331+3030" #s33 point 6, s34 point 7
#pointSrc="1411+5212" #s33 point 7, s34 point 6
#pointSrc="1153+8058" #s34 point 2
#pointSrc="0738+1742" #s34 point 3
#pointSrc="0854+5757" #s34 point 4
#pointSrc="0927+3902" # s34 point 5
#pointSrc="1023+3948" # s34 point 5 after 4:36
print "autoOOF source = ", oofSrc
print "flux source =  ", fluxSrc
print "point source = ", pointSrc

#----------------------------------------------------------------------
#               Nothing below here should be changed
#----------------------------------------------------------------------       

# location of project files
projectDir = "/home/astro-util/projects/gbt-edge"

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

# Argus Startup
# dfrayer 2017.08.01  17B Semester

##General Fix to 18.2 M&C system
##Resets all configuration values to defaults
##important after KFPA projects using frequency dictionary
ResetConfig()

# Startup the insrument by calling the 'presets' command
# This will turn on LNA/CIF if necessary
SetValues("RcvrArray75_115",{"presets":"on"})

print "CIF Power:", GetValue("RcvrArray75_115","cif_power")
print "LNA Power:", GetValue("RcvrArray75_115","lna_power")

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = fluxSrc

# set the receiver in the scan coordinator to avoid errors
SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# configuring manually to avoid re-tuning
Configure(point_config) # configure the pointing at the frequency of the source.
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(source)

Balance()

# pointing
AutoPeak(source,configure=False) # This peaks at the frequency of the source.

Break("enter pointing offsets")

# focusing
Focus(source) 

Break("enter focus values if necessary")

# nosc=22.0
# #map_radius = 2.8 # arcminutes

# daisyScanDuration = nosc * radial_osc_period / n_scans
# phi2 = 2.0 * nosc /n_scans
# phi1 = 3.14159265 * phi2

# #         -- increment radial_phase by phi1 each scan

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

 SCRIPT NUMBER 12, project:AGBT21B_024_37 
 288732 1090 Tony Wong 5 David Rose 2023-11-19 04:46:30 obs_completed 
#######################################################
#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs

#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "Mapping galaxy: ", galaxyName
print "Integration time per row (s): ", mymap['scanDuration']
print "Offset between map rows (arcsec): ", mymap['step']
print "Length of scan (arcmin): ", mymap['scanLength']
print "Height of map (arcmin): ", mymap['mapHeight']

Configure(argus_config)
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(galaxyName)
Balance()

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

DecLatMap( galaxyName,
           Offset("J2000", mymap['mapHeight']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['scanLength']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", mymap['step']/3600., 0.0, cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13


execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs

Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

           Offset("J2000", mymap['scanLength']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0,  mymap['mapHeight']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['step']/3600., cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

# location of project files

# Load in relevant catalogs
Catalog(qband_pointing)
Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(fluxcal)
c = Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "observing source:",  galaxyName, "at ", c[galaxyName]['location']

# set up configuration file and mapping parameters

# backend configuration
configFile = projectDir+"/12co.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# pointing configuration 
# If we're going to point at X-band don't need this. Leaving in place just in case.
configFile = projectDir+"/pointfocus.config" 
execfile(configFile)

# map setup 
mymap = {}
mymap['step'] = 2.6471 # arcsec
mymap['scanDuration'] = 33.0645 # s
mymap['nrows'] = 35
mymap['scanLength'] = 1.5 # arcmin
mymap['mapHeight'] = 1.5 # arcmin

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.7

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

           Offset("J2000", mymap['scanLength']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0,  mymap['mapHeight']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['step']/3600., cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

#load catalogs

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig()
